//18*SOwl - 机械斯坦 3D_SOwl - Maschinenstein 3D
ATTENTION: FOR THE GAME TO WORK PROPERLY, THE GRAVITY SHOULD BE SET TO 0! (Go to Enviroment on the bottom left corner and set gravity to 0)=注意：为了让游戏正常运行，重力应设置为 O！（前往左下角的环境设置并将重力设为 0）
To generate the level, I HIGLY RECOMMEND making it while the game is in slow motion!=为了生成关卡，我强烈建议在游戏处于慢动作状态下进行！
Change controls=更改控制
Go forward=前进
Fire=开火
Turn left=左转
Turn right=右转
Go backward=后退
Plot=剧情
You are a human. Just a human from the People Playground. Somehow, you appeared on this arena, and now you need to fight for your life. Why? Who knows, but you think that somewhere, there is another person, who watches you fighting, just for fun. So either kill, or you die.=你是一个人类.只是来自《人类游乐场》的普通人.不知为何,你出现在了这个竞技场上,现在你必须为生存而战.为什么?谁知道呢,但你认为在某个地方,有另一个人正在看着你战斗,仅仅是为了取乐.所以要么杀掉对方,要么你死.
Game guide=游戏教程
Note: this is only a demo version of what this system is capable of, so you may (I guess you will) encouter bugs=注意：这仅仅是该系统能力的演示版本，因此你可能会（我猜你一定会）遇到错误.
To play, first set amount of health (each dot represents 3 health points), amount of walls and amount of enemies=要开始游戏，首先设置生命值（每个点代表3点生命值）、墙体数量和敌人数量
After that, press button in the bottom of the start screen, and wait until the level is generated (15 seconds), but I HIGLY RECOMMEND making it while the game is in slow motion=之后，按下开始屏幕底部的按钮，等待关卡生成（15秒），但我强烈建议在游戏慢动作模式下进行.
Then, after the second screen appeared, press any buttons that are used in the game, and then kill all enemies.=然后，在第二个屏幕出现后，按下游戏中使用的任何按钮，然后杀死所有敌人.
Because the rendering system is a bit stupid, one enemy may be showed as many (but only visually)=因为渲染系统有点笨，一个敌人可能会显示为多个（但仅是视觉上）\
Note: the game is actually hard, just to understand where enemy is is already hard=注意：游戏实际上很难，光是弄清楚敌人在哪里就已经很难了.
You of course can spam the fire button=当然，你可以狂按开火键.
You shoot in both middle pixels, because of that the aim point looks like ++=你在两个中间像素处射击，因此瞄准点看起来像 ++.
After that, if you kill all enemies, you win! And you will lose if you lost all your hp.=在此之后，如果你杀死了所有敌人，你就赢了！如果你失去了所有生命值，你就会失败.
Also, if you don't kill all enemies within 2 minutes, all walls exept of the arena borders, if you still won't be able to find enemies, then sowwy, the game broke (just respawn it)=此外，如果你在2分钟内没有杀死所有敌人，除竞技场边界外的所有墙壁都会...如果你仍然找不到敌人，那么抱歉，游戏出错了（只需重新生成它）.
There is also a problem with the health, it may be showed wrongly, but the true amount of health is still right=生命值也存在一个问题，它可能显示错误，但真实的生命值仍然是正确的
The generation of the level is sometimes broken too, sowwy, but, if you will generate the game in slow motion the chance of it will decrease.=关卡的生成有时也会出问题，抱歉，但是，如果你在慢动作模式下生成游戏，出问题的几率会降低.
Amount of health=生命值数量
Amount of walls=墙体数量
Amount of enemies=敌人数量
Start the game=开始游戏
Activate the green lights to press button, or use bricks on the left if you can't activate them)=激活绿灯以按下按钮，或者如果你无法激活它们，则使用左侧的砖块.
I spent over 2 months making this game, so I will hope you will like it!=我花了两个多月制作这个游戏，所以我希望你会喜欢它！
Made by SOwl, with pain, hate, regret, and love!=由SOwl制作，伴随着痛苦、仇恨、悔恨与爱！
Also, PLEASE KEEP DISTANCE FROM WALLS OR ENEMIES, OTHERWISE YOU WILL GET THE "TOO MANY ACTIVATION SIGNALS" AND THE GAME WILL BREAK=另外，请与墙壁或敌人保持距离，否则你会收到“过多激活信号”并且游戏将崩溃.
Game actually works on both 1.27 and 1.28, so yeah enjoy!=游戏实际上在1.27和1.28版本上都能运行，所以尽情享受吧！
Game works on 32 iterations, but may also work on lower iterations, but maybe not as stable, but it will significantly improve your fps. (To change iteration, go to settings -> general -> Physics iteration count and change the thing=游戏在32次迭代下运行，但可能在更低迭代下也能运行，不过可能没那么稳定，但会显著提高你的FPS. （要更改迭代次数，请前往设置 -> 通用 -> 物理迭代计数并更改该数值）.
Game works kinda stable on 16 iterations, and works on 8. But i still recommend using 32 iterations if your CPU can handle the game=游戏在16次迭代下运行较为稳定，在8次迭代下也能运行. 但如果你的CPU能处理，我仍然建议使用32次迭代.
There are some visual errors because of the gazillion vires, so some parts that should not be transperent look like transperent, I can't fix it.=由于无数的线路，出现了一些视觉错误，所以一些本不该透明的部分看起来却是透明的，我无法修复它.
I will not change this version of the game (except for bug fixes), but you of course can write your suggestions to the next version of the game.=我不会更改游戏的这个版本（除了修复错误），但你当然可以为游戏的下一版本写下你的建议.
The whole magic happens in those black things, you can look what happens there, but I will post (or already posted) a guide about how I made it. Check the item Steam Workshop=所有的魔法都发生在那些黑色的东西里，你可以看看那里发生了什么，但我会发布（或已经发布了）一个关于我是如何制作它的指南.查看物品 Steam 创意工坊.
Generating level...=正在生成关卡...
Health=生命值
Enemies left=剩余敌人
Time=时间
Health on start=开始时的生命值
Health in the end=结束时的生命值
Enemy amount on start=开始时的敌人数
Enemy remain=敌人剩余数
You won!=你赢了！
You lost.=你输了.
To play again, clear everything and resapwn the contraption again=要重新开始，清除所有物品并重新生成该装置.

//43*表情人类
Harder, Better, Faster, Stronger of the first part. Optimizated!=第一部分更艰难、更好、更快、更强. 已优化！
We have prepared a trailer for this long-awaited mod. Would you like to take a look? I think you'll like it.=我们为这个期待已久的模组准备了一个预告片. 你想看看吗？我想你会喜欢的
The first part of the mod was created by me when I was just starting to understand modding. The mod has been completely rewritten, redrawn, modified, optimized.\nI want to say thank you to everyone who worked on this mod. I also want to inform you that the mod can cause lags in weak computers, but for this I have provided an outcome.\nIn the folder People Playground/Mods/01STUDIO/HDE2/settings.json you can change the cycle time.\nThe larger it is, the less frequently the emotion will be updated, the fewer operations your computer will perform.\n\nAll this is explained in the trailer, so you can watch it by finding it on the channel.=模组的第一部分是我刚开始学习模组制作时创建的. 该模组已被完全重写、重绘、修改和优化.\n我想感谢所有参与此模组制作的人. 同时我也想告知你，该模组在性能较弱的电脑上可能会导致卡顿，但为此我提供了一个解决方案. \n在 People Playground/Mods/01STUDIO/HDE2/settings.json 文件夹中，你可以更改循环时间.\n该值越大，情绪更新的频率就越低，你的电脑执行的操作也就越少.\n\n所有这些在预告片中都有解释，你可以在频道上找到并观看.
<b>Human Dynamic Emotions 2</b>\r\nHuman that expresses his feeling in whatever stuff he feels.=<b>人类动态情绪2</b>\r\n一个会以他感受到的任何事物来表达自己情感的人类.

//45*更强的爆炸冲击波_Better Explosion Shockwaves
Explosion Shockwaves=爆炸冲击波
Spawn the "Toggle Explosion Shockwaves" item to enable shockwaves, located in the Entities tab\nRecommended to play on slow-motion\nThe shockwaves shouldnt be too laggy, if it is, turn off Fancy Effects\n  The mod is labeled as suspicious because I had to use "GetField" and "UserPreferencesManager" to be able to tell if you have Fancy Effects on.=生成位于“实体”栏中的“切换爆炸冲击波”物品以启用冲击波.\n建议在慢动作模式下游玩.\n冲击波不应该太卡，如果卡，请关闭“精致特效”.\n  该模组被标记为可疑，因为我不得不使用“GetField”和“UserPreferencesManager”来判断你是否开启了“精致特效”.
<b>Shockwave Emitter</b>\r\nEmits a customizable shockwave when activated.=<b>冲击波发射器</b>\r\n激活时发射可定制的冲击波.
<b>Toggle Explosion Shockwaves</b>\r\nSpawn me! Toggles whether or not all spawned explosives should have realistic shockwaves. Turn off fancy effects in the settings for a lower quality shockwave.=<b>切换爆炸冲击波</b>\r\n生成我！切换是否让所有生成的爆炸物都具有逼真的冲击波. 在设置中关闭华丽效果可获得较低质量的冲击波.
Explosion shockwaves have been disabled for every explosive!=每个爆炸物的爆炸冲击波已禁用!
Explosion shockwaves have been enabled for every explosive!=每个爆炸物的爆炸冲击波已启用!
Set Shockwave Force=设置冲击波力度
Set Dismember Chance=设置肢解几率
Set Particle count=设置粒子数量
Toggle Shockwave Rebound=切换冲击波反弹
Set Shockwave Force.=设置冲击波力度.
Set Dismember Chance.=设置肢解几率.
Set Particle count.=设置粒子数量.
Toggle Shockwave Rebound.=切换冲击波反弹.
Total shockwave rebound has been set to: True=总冲击波反弹已设置为：开启
Total shockwave rebound has been set to: False=总冲击波反弹已设置为：关闭
Add Explosion Shockwave=添加爆炸冲击波
Add Explosion Shockwave.=添加爆炸冲击波.





//46*悬停观测 
Hover Inspector=悬停观测
Modify keybinds in config.json. Shows inspect menu of a person when hovered over automatically. Aims to be lightweight and minimal to allow maximum performance and mod compatibility.=在 config.json 中修改按键绑定. 鼠标悬停时自动显示人物的观测面板. 旨在轻量化、最小化，以实现最高性能和模组兼容性.(默认左Alt)
Inspect on Hover Permanence: False=悬停观测永久性：关闭
Inspect on Hover Permanence: True=悬停观测永久性：开启

//55*高级物理
Advanced Physics=高级物理
Advanced physics settings and increased physics accuracy.=高级物理设置与更高的物理精度.
<b>Dynamic Force Drag</b>\n[Advanced Physics] A drag tool that scales applied force with Physics FPS.=<b>动态力拖拽</b>\n[高级物理] 拖拽力度随物理帧率自动缩放，保证任何帧率下拖拽感觉都一样.

//设置
[Advanced Physics] Physics FPS=[高级物理] 物理帧率
[Advanced Physics] Slow Motion Scaling=[高级物理] 慢动作缩放

How many times will physics update in a second. Higher value %3D better accuracy, worse performance, possible instability; Lower value %3D worse accuracy, better performance.\nVanilla value: 50 | Default value: 150 (Recommended)=每秒物理更新次数. 值越高%3D精度越高，性能越差，可能不稳定\n值越低%3D精度越差，性能越好. 	原版：50 | 默认值：150（推荐）

0 %3D Slow Motion doesn't affect Physics FPS (Vanilla); Gives FPS boost while in Slow Mo. 1 %3D Physics Updates rate fully scales with Slow Mo, meaning physics improves the slower the game is; FPS doesn't change while in Slow Mo. =0 %3D 慢动作不影响物理FPS（原版）；在慢动作中FPS会更好. \n1 %3D 物理更新率完全随慢动作缩放，意味着游戏越慢物理精度越高；在慢动作中FPS不会更好.

Number of physical properties packets per second (temperature, charge)=每秒物理属性数据包数量（温度、电荷）

Number of entity packets per second (health, consciousness, pain, etc.)=每秒实体数据包数量（生命值、意识、疼痛等）


























//57*场景动画
Stop-motion keyframe animator. Freeze the map, pose ragdolls without dismembering them, capture frames, and play them back with Smooth / Linear / EaseInOut / Bounce / Stepped / Choppy modes. Press F6 to open, F7 to capture, F8 to play.=定格动画关键帧动画器. 冻结地图，摆弄布娃娃而不肢解它们，捕捉帧，并以平滑/线性/缓入缓出/弹跳/步进/跳跃模式回放. 按F6打开，F7捕捉，F8播放.

SCOPE=范围
People=人类
SCOPE: capture & animate only characters.=范围：仅捕捉和动画角色.
Environ.=环境
SCOPE: capture & animate only items / the world (not people).=范围：仅捕捉和动画物品/世界（不包括人类）.
Everything=所有物体
SCOPE: capture & animate everything in the scene.=范围：捕捉和动画场景中的所有物体.

STAGE=演出
Freeze Map=冻结地图
Unfreeze Map=取消冻结地图
Anchor the whole world so the background holds still while you pose. People stay grabbable. Click again to unfreeze.=锚定整个世界，使背景在你摆姿势时保持静止. 人物仍可抓取. 再次点击取消冻结.
Pin People=固定人类
Unpin People=取消固定人类
Hold every character frozen in place so a pose can't fall apart. Unpin to grab/pose them again.=将每个角色固定在原地，使姿势不会散架. 取消固定后可再次抓取/摆姿势.
Keep Alive ON=保持存活开启
Keep Alive=保持存活
Characters can't die while animating. Click to allow normal damage.=动画制作期间角色不会死亡. 点击允许正常伤害.

POSING=摆姿势
Nodes=节点
Nodes ON=节点开启
Show draggable circles on every joint. Drag a circle = rotate that bone; Shift+drag = move it.=在每个关节上显示可拖拽的圆圈. 拖拽圆圈 = 旋转该骨骼；Shift+拖拽 = 移动它.
Isolate=隔离
Click...=点击...
Then click ONE part - shows a single node for just that limb and its children.=然后点击一个部位 - 仅显示该肢体及其子部件的单个节点.
Snap 15=吸附15度
Free=自由
Rotation snaps to 15-degree steps. Click for free rotation.=旋转按15度步长吸附. 点击切换自由旋转.
Rotation is free (no snapping). Click to snap to 15 degrees.=旋转自由（无吸附）. 点击吸附到15度.
Exit=退出
Stop posing and unfreeze everything.=停止摆姿势并解冻所有物体.

CAMERA=相机
Camera Frame=相机框
Camera ON=相机开启
Show a movable / resizable / rotatable frame = the shot the animation camera will use. Drag edges to move, corners to size, top dot to rotate.=显示一个可移动/缩放/旋转的框 = 动画相机将使用的镜头. 拖拽边缘移动，拖拽角改变大小，拖拽顶部圆点旋转.
The camera frame is showing. Click to hide it.=相机框正在显示. 点击隐藏它.
Look Through=镜头跟随
Looking=跟随中
Move the real game camera to the frame - preview, and follow it during playback. Leave OFF if you don't want the camera to move.=将实际游戏相机移动到框的位置 - 预览，并在播放时跟随. 如果你不希望相机移动，请保持关闭.
The camera is following the frame. Click to stop.=相机正在跟随框. 点击停止.

r:"\s*Frame\s*(\d+)\s*\((\d+)p\)"=帧 $1 ($2p)
Capture=捕获
Snapshot the whole scene as a NEW keyframe.=将整个场景快照为一个新关键帧.
Rec=录制
REC=录制中
Auto-capture a keyframe every 'frame time' while you pose - and records any item you ACTIVATE so it re-fires on playback. Toggle.=在你摆姿势时每隔“帧时长”自动捕获一个关键帧 - 并记录你激活的任何物品，使其在播放时重新触发. 切换开关.
Recording - capturing frames + your item activations automatically. Click to stop.=录制中 - 自动捕获帧 + 你的物品激活. 点击停止.
Reverse=反转
Reverse the order of all frames.=反转所有帧的顺序.
Update=更新
Overwrite the selected frame with the current scene pose/camera.=用当前场景姿势/相机覆盖选中的帧.
Mark Fire=标记开火
Click item=点击物品
Then click a weapon/item - it will FIRE when playback reaches the selected frame. Mark across frames for held/full-auto.=然后点击武器/物品 - 当播放到达选中帧时它将开火. 跨帧标记可实现持续/全自动.
Mark Free=标记释放
Click part=点击部件
Then click a character (frees their WHOLE body + held items) or an item - it's released to physics at the selected frame and ragdolls free with the animation's momentum.=然后点击一个角色（释放其整个身体 + 手持物品）或一个物品 - 它在选中的帧被释放为物理，并带着动画的动量自由布娃娃化.
Clear=清除
Delete ALL frames.=删除所有帧.
r:"Frame (\d+)\s+\((\d+)p\)"=帧 $1   ($2p)
Prev=上一帧

Next=下一帧

Go To=跳转

Insert=插入

Dup=复制

Up=上移

PLAYBACK MODE=播放模式
Smooth=平滑
Playback: eased smooth motion between frames.=播放：帧之间的平滑缓动运动.
Linear=线性
Playback: constant-speed motion between frames.=播放：帧之间的匀速运动.
EaseInOut=缓入缓出
Playback: accelerate then decelerate between frames.=播放：帧之间先加速后减速.
Bounce=弹跳
Playback: bounce/overshoot at each frame.=播放：在每个帧处弹跳/过冲.
Stepped=步进
Playback: snap through N in-between steps (choppy but moving).=播放：通过N个中间步进快照（卡顿但移动）.
Choppy=跳跃
Playback: hard snap between frames (true stop-motion).=播放：帧之间硬切换（真正的定格动画）.

TIMING=计时

<b>AI Microchip</b>\r\n<color%3D#0095FF>A cybernetic implant for any <b>human</b> or <b>android</b><br><color%3D#55B8FF>NZT-48 chipset<br><color%3D#FF9500>This is <u>not</u> the real <b>NZT-48</b> chip, it is a replica created by <b>Charlie Gordon</b> from refurbished <b>MEOWZT-48</b> chips. His modifications have reclassified the chip as 'not just for cats'.=<b>AI 微芯片</b>\r\n<color%3D#0095FF>一种用于任何<b>人类</b>或<b>机器人</b>的义体植入物.<br><color%3D#55B8FF>NZT-48 芯片组.<br><color%3D#FF9500>这不是真正的 <b>NZT-48</b> 芯片，而是由 <b>查理·戈登</b> 用翻新的 <b>MEOWZT-48</b> 芯片制造的复制品. 他的改装使得该芯片被重新定义为“不仅限于猫”. 

<b>64K Memory</b>\r\nAdds 64K of RAM allowing AI to recognize people and things from their past.<br><br><color%3Dyellow>WARNING!<br><color%3Dred> May cause AI to remember things they wish they could forget.</color>.=<b>64K 内存</b>\r\n增加 64K 内存，使 AI 能够识别过去的人和事物.<br><br><color%3Dyellow>警告！<br><color%3Dred>可能导致 AI 回忆起它们希望遗忘的事情.</color> 

<b>Firearms Chip Upgrade</b>\r\n<color%3D#62FF63>This was a collaberation between <br><b>Gunnery Sergeant Hartman</b> & <b>Private Pyle</b>.<br><color%3D#41AA42>The chip implants an artificial medulla oblongata (AMO) allowing AI to kill without remorse yet show mercy to anyone that's weak sauce.=<b>枪械芯片升级</b>\r\n<color%3D#62FF63>这是由<b>枪炮中士哈特曼</b>与<b>二等兵派尔</b>合作的成果.<br><color%3D#41AA42>该芯片植入了一个人工延髓（AMO），使 AI 能够毫无悔意地杀戮，同时又能对那些弱鸡表现出怜悯. 

<b>Karate Chip Upgrade</b>\r\nThe official chip used by the <b><color%3D#C2BA7F>YMCA Tae Bo Club</b>.<br><color%3D#FF6263>Over 10,000 hours of MoCap data analyzed featuring <color%3D#FF9697>Michael Dudikoff</color> performing all 3 of <b><color%3D#62FF63>Chuck Norris'</color></b> legendary kicks.<br><color%3D#8D82FA>(tight jeans required to reach full potential)=<b>空手道芯片升级</b>\r\n<b><color%3D#C2BA7F>YMCA 跆搏俱乐部</b>使用的官方芯片.<br><color%3D#FF6263>分析了超过 10,000 小时的动作捕捉数据，由 <color%3D#FF9697>迈克尔·杜迪考夫</color> 表演了 <b><color%3D#62FF63>查克·诺里斯</color></b> 的全部三种传奇踢技.<br><color%3D#8D82FA>（需要紧身牛仔裤才能发挥全部潜力） 

<b>Melee Chip Upgrade</b>\r\n<color%3D#FF9500>Developed by the <b><color%3D##F6A00>Droogs</color></b> to glitch the effects of <color%3D#8D82FA>aversion therapy</color>.<br><br><color%3D#FFAD55>Infected AI seen prowling the streets looking to duff up any bloke with <color%3Dred><b>ultra-violence</b></color> and <color%3Dred><b>gusto</b>.=<b>近战芯片升级</b>\r\n<color%3D#FF9500>由<b><color%3D##F6A00>恶棍</color></b>开发，用于扰乱 <color%3D#8D82FA>厌恶疗法</color> 的效果.<br><br><color%3D#FFAD55>受感染的 AI 在街头游荡，寻找任何倒霉鬼，施以 <color%3Dred><b>极端暴力</b></color> 和 <color%3Dred><b>狂热暴行</b>.

//73*快捷键姿势_Quick Turn On Poses
Quick Turn On Poses=快捷键姿势
Use the U + I,O,L,LeftBracket,RightBracket key combination to activate the human animations.=使用 U + I、O、L、左方括号、右方括号的组合键来激活人类动画.
Pose: Modifier key=姿态：组合键/重置姿势
Pose: Walk=姿态：行走
Pose: Cower=姿态：蜷缩
Pose: Sit=姿态：正坐
Pose: Stumble=姿态：蹒跚
Pose: Flat=姿态：直立

//75*现代枪械模组_Modern Firearms Mod
Modern Firearms=现代枪械
It contains the most advanced firearms in its class.=它包含了同类中最先进的枪械.
<color%3D#FABF7E>Check <color%3Dgreen>the Context Menu for</color> special functions!</color>=<color%3D#FABF7E>查看右键菜单中的</color><color%3Dgreen>特殊功能！</color>
NO Ammo=无弹药
Reloaded=换弹
Reset Gun=重置枪械
Reset gun back to factory settings.=将枪械重置为出厂设置.
Switched to <color%3Dgreen>Auto=切换到<color%3Dgreen>全自动模式
Semi-Auto=半自动模式
Switch shooting mode to semi-auto.=将射击模式切换为半自动.
Switched to <color%3D#FABF7E>Semi-auto=切换到<color%3D#FABF7E>半自动模式
Limited Ammo=有限弹药
<color%3Dred>Makes them limited. To make it with each gun on spawn Press [L]</color>=<color%3Dred>使弹药变为有限. 要让每把枪在生成时都带有此效果，请按 [L]</color>
Limited Ammo HIDE=隐藏弹药数
<color%3Dwhite>The same limited amount of ammo only without pop-up messages. Useful if you are shooting a video or film. To make it with each gun on spawn Press [H]</color>=<color%3Dwhite>相同的有限弹药数量，但没有弹出消息. 如果你正在拍摄视频或电影，这很有用. 要让每把枪在生成时都带有此效果，请按 [H]</color>
Show Ammo=显示弹药数
<color%3Dred>Shows your current ammo.</color>=<color%3Dred>显示你当前的弹药. </color>
Reload Ammo=重新换弹
<color%3Dwhite>Reload if no ammo. To reload each gun on spawn Press [U]</color>=<color%3Dwhite>弹药不足时重新装填. 要让每把枪在生成时都自动装填，请按 [U]</color>
Infinity Ammo=无限弹药
<color%3Dred>Makes them infinity. To make it with each gun on spawn Press [I]</color>=<color%3Dred>使弹药变为无限. 要让每把枪在生成时都带有此效果，请按 [I]</color>

//77*平滑相机_Smooth Camera | QoL Mod
Smooth Camera Pan=平滑镜头平移
Replaces the default middle-mouse camera drag with a smooth, eased pan. Hold middle mouse and drag to glide the view around. Scroll-zoom is unaffected.=用平滑、缓动的平移替换默认的中键相机拖拽. 按住鼠标中键并拖动以滑动视图. 滚动缩放不受影响(菜单F9)
Smooth Camera=平滑相机.
Smoothing: ON=平滑：开启
Smoothing: OFF=平滑：关闭
Smoothness: =平滑度：
F9 to hide/show=F9 隐藏/显示.













//78*缓慢滚轮_Slow-Mo Dial - Shift + Scrollwheel 
Hold Shift and scroll to dial time from paused (0%) to fast-forward (200%). Zoom is suppressed while Shift is held so scrolling only controls time.=按住 Shift 并滚动，可将时间从暂停（0%）调整到快进（200%）. 按住 Shift 期间，缩放功能被禁用，因此滚动仅用于控制时间(菜单F8)

//82*幽灵附身模组_Spectral Possession
Spectral Possession=幽灵附身
Summon orbs that attach to humans or androids and can grant themed powers.=召唤能够附着在人类或机器人上并赋予主题能力的球体.
<b>Possession</b>\r\nOrbs you can bind to humans or androids. Many powers spread through lower-arm contact; androids use their own glow and eye sprites. Combine different orbs to blend traits, merge identical orbs for stronger faster contact powers, or use the Orb Absorber to keep unlimited absorbed types. Hold F while your lower arms touch another person (touching them anywhere on the body) to move the spirit; elemental and passive orb effects pause until you finish charging. Forearms glow while you charge the transfer.=<b>附身</b>\r\n你可以将球体绑定到人类或机器人上. 许多能力通过前臂接触传播; 机器人会使用自己的发光和眼部精灵. 组合不同的球体以混合特性, 合并相同的球体以获得更强更快的接触能力, 或者使用球体吸收器来保留无限的吸收类型. 在前臂接触另一个人（触碰其身体任何部位）时按住 F 键可移动灵魂; 元素和被动球体效果会暂停, 直到你完成充能. 充能传输时前臂会发光.
<b>Regular Orb</b>\r\nSimple possession: no special passive, no elemental effect, and no powers that spread from the host's lower arms to others.=<b>普通灵球</b>\r\n简单的附身：没有特殊被动，没有元素效果，也没有通过宿主下臂传播给其他人的能力.
<b>Immortal Orb</b>\r\nMakes the host very hard to injure or kill.=<b>不朽灵球</b>\r\n使宿主极难受伤或死亡.
<b>Undead Orb</b>\r\nMakes the host undead. Lower-arm contact with other humans spreads the infection. Androids cannot be turned.=<b>亡灵灵球</b>\r\n使宿主变为亡灵. 与其他人类下臂接触会传播感染. 机器人无法被转化.
<b>Healing Orb</b>\r\nSlow, steady healing for the host. Lost limbs do not regrow. Lower-arm contact can help stabilize or revive other people who are badly hurt.=<b>治愈灵球</b>\r\n为宿主提供缓慢而稳定的治疗. 失去的肢体不会再生. 下臂接触可以帮助稳定或复活重伤的其他人类.
<b>Electrical Orb</b>\r\nThe host readily conducts electricity. Sustained lower-arm contact shocks anyone the host keeps touching.=<b>电力灵球</b>\r\n宿主易于导电. 持续的下臂接触会对宿主触碰的任何对象造成电击.
<b>Fire Orb</b>\r\nProtects the host from burning. Lower-arm contact can ignite other people the host is holding on to.=<b>火焰灵球</b>\r\n保护宿主不被烧焦. 下臂接触可以点燃宿主接触到的其他人.
<b>Acid Orb</b>\r\nClears acid from the host. Lower-arm contact deals strong acid damage to anyone in contact.=<b>强酸灵球</b>\r\n清除宿主身上的酸液. 下臂接触会对接触到的任何人造成强酸伤害.
<b>Frost Orb</b>\r\nProtects the host from freezing. Lower-arm contact chills other people and can eventually freeze the limbs the host is touching.=<b>寒霜灵球</b>\r\n保护宿主不被冻结. 下臂接触会使其他人变冷，最终冻结宿主接触到的肢体.
<b>Blood Orb</b>\r\nSteadies the host's blood flow. Lower-arm contact draws blood from other people into the host.=<b>鲜血灵球</b>\r\n稳定宿主的血液流动. 下臂接触将其他人的血液吸入宿主体内.
<b>Poison Orb</b>\r\nClears rot and poison on the host. Lower-arm contact can make another person sick for a long time.=<b>毒素灵球</b>\r\n清除宿主身上的腐烂和毒素. 下臂接触可使另一个人长时间生病.
<b>Disintegrate Orb</b>\r\nAffects only the host, human or android: the body rots and falls apart. Does not spread through the air or through the host's arms; only that body takes damage.=<b>崩解灵球</b>\r\n仅影响宿主（人类或机器人）：身体会腐烂并瓦解. 不会通过空气或宿主的手臂传播；只有宿主身体会受到伤害.
<b>Rupture Orb</b>\r\nAffects only the host: bleeding, shock, and pain keep spiking. No free-air or arm-spread effect; damage stays inside the host's body.=<b>撕裂灵球</b>\r\n仅影响宿主：失血、休克和疼痛持续飙升. 没有空气传播或手臂扩散效果；伤害只停留在宿主体内.
<b>Orb Absorber</b>\r\nAbsorbs unlimited other orbs and keeps all of their powers. Collide with possessed humans to steal the spirit to a new body.=<b>灵球吸收器</b>\r\n吸收无限的其他灵球并保留它们的所有力量. 与被附身的人类碰撞可将灵魂窃取至新的身体.
Unpossess=解除附身
Detach the orb and make the host collapse again.=分离球体并让宿主再次倒下.

//89*分类排序_Category Sorting Mod
Category Sorting Mod=分类排序模组
This is a Category Sorting mod, this Mod Sorts Categories with custom 'Side' Categories by showing only the stuff you need, a UI is added near the catalog where the side categories are, this could also lag or mess something up if you mess with it=这是一个分类排序模组，它通过只显示你需要的内容来对带有自定义“侧边”分类进行分类，一个用户界面被添加到目录附近侧边分类所在的位置，如果你胡乱操作，这也可能会导致卡顿或出现问题

//91*哈利波特
Includes 120+ Humans, Creatures, and Objects from the Wizarding World of Harry Potter!=包括 120 多种来自哈利·波特魔法世界的人类、生物和物品！
<b>Harry Potter Power Pack</b>\r\nContains many iconic characters from the movies, books, and games set in the wizarding world of Harry Potter - Team Wilson.=<b>哈利·波特能力包[TF_RC汉化]</b>\r\n包含来自电影、书籍和游戏中众多基于哈利·波特魔法世界的标志性角色 - Wilson团队.


//魔法书
Spell Book=魔法书
Spell Book.=魔法书.
Close Book=关闭书本
Choose=选择

Lumos=荧光闪烁
A spell that illuminated the tip of the caster's wand, allowing the caster to see in the dark.=一种能使魔杖尖端发光的咒语，让施咒者在黑暗中看清事物. 

Expecto Patronum=呼神护卫
This spell is a highly powerful and advanced protective spell which will conjure a spirit guardian of their positive emotions to defend against dark creatures=这是一个极其强大且高级的保护咒，能召唤出由施咒者积极情绪构成的灵魂守护者，用以抵御黑暗生物

Leviosa=羽加迪姆勒维奥萨
A charm that levitated objects. However, it did not also allow one to move said objects=一种使物体漂浮的魔咒，但并不能移动该物体

Accio=飞来咒
Also known as the summoning charm, it was a charm that summoned an object toward the caster. It was able to summon objects in direct line of sight of the caster, if the wand was pointed at the object.=也被称为召唤咒，能将物体召唤到施咒者身边. 如果魔杖对准物体且在直接视线内，即可召唤. 

Sectumsempra=神锋无影
A curse invented by Professor Severus Snape that lacerates the target and causes severe haemorrhaging. Snape created it as a student of Hogwarts, with the intention of using it against his enemies.=由西弗勒斯·斯内普教授发明的诅咒，能撕裂目标并造成严重出血. 斯内普在霍格沃茨读书时创造此咒，意在对付敌人. 

Wilsonmorphosis=威尔逊变形咒
The deadliest curse of all, made by Lord Wilson. It has the power to use living organisms as a host to give birth to Lord Wilson's victims, causing excruciating pain to the victim before their insides explode and Lord Wilson's minions are born.=由威尔逊勋爵创造的最致命诅咒. 它能以活物为宿主，孕育出威尔逊勋爵的受害者，使宿主在极度痛苦中内脏爆裂，继而诞生威尔逊的仆从. 

Wilsoniferous Exterminatus=威尔逊灭绝咒
A curse created by the Dark Lord Wilson that will cause his minions to all converge on one human. The minions will destroy everything in their way until they reach and destroy their target.=黑魔王威尔逊创造的诅咒，能让他的所有仆从集中攻击一个人类. 仆从们会摧毁路上的一切，直到抵达并消灭目标. 

Wilsoniarmada Bombardium=威尔逊军械轰炸咒
Causes all of Lord Wilson's Minions to spontaneously combust. This attack was used during the third wizarding world to turn the tides of the war in Wilson's favor.=使威尔逊勋爵的所有仆从自爆. 此攻击曾在第三次巫师战争中使用，扭转战局，使威尔逊占上风. 

Inflatus=膨胀咒
A charm, or sometimes referred to as a jinx, which when focused on an object or living being, would inflate it to the point it would burst.=一种魔咒（有时也被称为恶咒），当对准物体或生物时，会使其膨胀直至爆裂. 

Protego=盔甲护身
A spell that when activated, it will Cause a moderately sized orb to emit from the tip of the wand. The orb can be used to stop most spells, except for more powerful spells.=激活时，魔杖尖端会发射出一个中等大小的球体. 该球体可阻挡大多数咒语，但无法抵挡更强大的咒语. 

Arresto Momentum=减震止速
A spell that could be used to slow the velocity of an object. very useful to immobilize enemies, or to slow the fall of a person.=一种能减缓物体速度的咒语. 非常适合定住敌人或减缓人的下落速度. 

Petrificus Totalus=统统石化
Also known as the Body Freezing Spell, was a curse that temporarily paralysed the opponent, it did not actually freeze the victim in ice. It was often used by inexperienced or young wizards and witches in duelling.=也被称为“身体冻结咒”，是一种暂时瘫痪对手的诅咒，实际上并不会将受害者冻在冰里. 它常被缺乏经验或年轻的巫师在决斗中使用. 

Crucio=钻心剜骨
Also known as the Torture Curse, it was a tool of the Dark Arts and one of the three Unforgivable Curses. When cast successfully on a living creature, the curse inflicted intense, excruciating physical pain on the victim.=也被称为“酷刑咒”，是黑魔法工具之一，三大不可饶恕咒之一. 成功施咒后，会给活物带来剧烈而难以忍受的肉体痛苦. 

Melofors=南瓜头咒
also known as the Pumpkin-Head Jinx, it was a jinx that encased the victim's head in a pumpkin. To outsiders, it appeared that the victim's head was transformed into a pumpkin.=也被称为“南瓜头恶咒”，是一种将受害者头部封入南瓜中的恶咒. 从外人看来，受害者的脑袋似乎变成了南瓜. 

Geminio=复制成双
A spell used to curse an object into multiplying repeatedly when touched. This spell was useful to protect valuables and trap the perpitrator. Note: Causes lag when too many items are spawned=一种用于诅咒物品的咒语，使物品在被触碰时不断复制. 该咒语有助于保护贵重物品并困住作案者. 注意：复制过多物体会导致卡顿

Expelliarmus=除你武器
The Disarming Charm was a charm that forced whatever an opponent was holding to fly out of their hand. It was common to see this spell used in duels to make an opponent lose their wand.=缴械咒，能迫使对手手中所持之物飞脱. 该咒常在决斗中使用，以使对手失去魔杖. 

Avada Kedavra=阿瓦达索命
The Killing Curse was a tool of the Dark Arts and was one of the three Unforgivable Curses. When cast successfully on a living being, the curse caused instantaneous and painless death, without causing any injury to the body, and without any trace of violence.=杀戮咒是黑魔法工具之一，三大不可饶恕咒之一. 成功施咒后，会使活物瞬间无痛死亡，身体不留任何伤痕，也无暴力痕迹. 

Glacius=冰冻咒
A charm that froze a target with icy-cold air created from the tip of the wand. This, in turn, could freeze living beings, cool down burning objects or machinery, etc.=一种用魔杖尖端发出的冰冷空气冻结目标的魔咒. 由此可冻结生物、冷却燃烧的物体或机械等

Stupefy=昏迷咒
A charm that stunned the target, rendering them unconscious. This charm was exceptionally useful in duelling, as it can quickly end a duel without causing lasting damage.=一种使目标眩晕、失去知觉的魔咒. 该咒在决斗中极其有用，能快速结束决斗且不造成持久伤害. 

Rennervate=复苏咒
a charm that awakened an unconscious target. Consequently, it served as the counter-charm to the Stupify Spell, the Petrificus Totalus Spell, and can negate the effects caused by directly staring into a Basilisk's gaze.=一种唤醒昏迷目标的魔咒. 因此，它是昏迷咒、统统石化咒的反咒，也能抵消直视蛇怪眼睛所造成的影响. 

Bombarda=爆炸咒
Bombarda was a spell that detonated the target in a small explosion. It is a useful spell for destroying objects.=爆炸咒是一种以小型爆炸引爆目标的咒语. 对于摧毁物体十分有用. 

Incendio=火焰咒
A spell that conjured a jet of flames that could be used to set things alight, including living things. This spell is very useful for arson on architecture or humans.=一种能召唤火焰喷射的咒语，可用于点燃物体，包括生物. 此咒对纵火建筑或人类非常有用. 

Fumos=烟雾咒
A charm used to create a defensive cloud of smoke from the wand that hindered visibility. This spell was quite useful in duelling, as the smoke hid the caster, preventing an opponent from accurately aiming their spells, as well as allowing the caster to escape unseen.=一种从魔杖尖端产生防御性烟雾云以阻碍视线的魔咒. 此咒在决斗中非常有用，烟雾能隐藏施咒者，使对手无法准确瞄准咒语，同时让施咒者得以不被察觉地逃脱.

//103*隐形_Anything invisible
Anything invisible (Upgraded)=隐形一切 (更新)
Adds a way to make items and or effects invisible (without breaking detail view). It also automatically fixes all spawned items that would normally break detail view (because the old mod made items save improperly)=提供了一种使物品和/或效果隐形（且不破坏详情视图）的方法. 它还会自动修复所有通常会在详情视图中出现问题的已生成物品（因为旧模组导致物品保存不当）
<color%3D#fad9ff>Add Invisibility</color>=<color%3D#fad9ff>添加隐身</color>
Gives the invisible component and makes it invisible=赋予不可见组件并使其隐形
Gives the invisible component and makes it invisible.=赋予不可见组件并使其隐形.
r:"Added invisibility to (.*)\."=已向 $1 添加隐身效果. 
<color%3D#fad9ff>Remove Invisibility</color>=<color%3D#fad9ff>移除隐身</color>
Destroys the invisible component=销毁不可见组件.
Destroys the invisible component.=销毁不可见组件. 
r:"Removed invisibility from (.*)\."=已从 $1 移除隐身效果. 
<color%3D#fad9ff>Disable DetailView Visibility</color>=<color%3D#fad9ff>禁用详情视图可见性</color>
<color%3D#fad9ff>Enable DetailView Visibility</color>=<color%3D#fad9ff>启用详情视图可见性</color>
<color%3D#fad9ff>Toggle DetailView Visibility</color>=<color%3D#fad9ff>切换详情视图可见性</color>
Toggles visibility in detail view=在详情视图中切换可见性
Toggles visibility in detail view.=在详情视图中切换可见性.
r:"(.*) is now visible in detail view\."=$1 现在在详情视图中可见.
r:"(.*) is now invisible in detail view\."=$1 现在在详情视图中不可见.
<color%3D#fad9ff>Remove Effects</color>=<color%3D#fad9ff>移除效果</color>
Removes non-physical visuals that save with the item. It should be noted that you can't undo removals. <color%3D#fad9ff>Extra effects get added to the 'save list' allowing more changes to be saved in vanilla, but require adding them to the list each time before saving/copying (e.g.; copy-paste-copy-paste item and you'll see extra effects aren't removed anymore)</color>=移除随物品保存的非物理视觉效果. 请注意，移除操作无法撤销. <color%3D#fad9ff>额外效果会被添加到“保存列表”，允许在原版中保存更多改动，但每次保存/复制前都需要将其添加到列表（例如：复制-粘贴-复制-粘贴物品，你会发现额外效果不再被移除）</color>
r:"Removed basic decals from (.*)\."=已从 $1 移除基础贴花. 
r:"(.*) added to serialization list"=$1 已添加到序列化列表. 
r:"Removed (\d+) effect/s from (.*)\."=已从 $2 移除 $1 个效果.

//107*念力
Touch the Psy Orb (Entities tab) to a person to grant TELEKINESIS! Right-click them to control their powers. ATTACK MODE turns them into an autonomous hunter that floats around attacking anyone nearby - hurling objects, ripping open walls to reach people hiding inside, tearing victims in half, disarming gunmen and turning their own guns on them, slamming bodies into the ground, and flipping entire vehicles - while defending itself with a deflect field that throws attacks back and a curved debris shield that blocks gunfire. MANUAL MODE gives you full control: fly with WASD and aim every power yourself - grab and throw objects, home a gun onto an enemy's head, flip occupied vehicles, and smash two people together. Works on any human or android.=将念力球（位于实体标签页）拖到一个人身上，即可赋予其念力！右键点击他们可控制其能力. 攻击模式会将其变成一个自主猎手，漂浮在空中攻击附近的任何人——投掷物体、撕开墙壁以攻击藏在里面的人、将目标撕成两半、缴械枪手并使其枪口转向自己、将人猛砸向地面、掀翻整个载具——同时利用偏转场弹回攻击，并利用弯曲的碎片盾阻挡枪弹. 手动模式则让你完全掌控：使用WASD飞行并亲自瞄准每一种能力——抓取并投掷物体、引导枪械瞄准敌人的头部、掀翻有人的载具、将两个人猛撞在一起. 适用于任何人类或机器人.

<b>The Utopia Enemies Detected (TUED)</b>\r\nHuge Ramaster Of The Original Utopia Mod.=<b>乌托邦敌人检测 (TUED)[TF_RC汉化]</b>\r\n原乌托邦模组的巨大重制版


<b>[Project Paragon] Last Part - TUED</b>\r\nThe greatest collaboration project between DISKIO.inc and V.L.A.S.T. The best engineers and scientists from both sides, led by Kapitel, were creating a powerful weapon capable of stopping the violence and retaking the old lands. Due to the incredible power of the core inside him, Paragon is able to annihilate everything with its laser, and also able to create incredibly powerful electrical storms to destroy massive areas. Paragon also has the ability to disintegrate everything around him, causing void anomalies by using extremely powerful processors in his head. Everything was fine, but one day the resistance was able to successfully sabotage construction of the Paragon, which caused its destruction in the process. Probably it can be restored and finished, but you'll need to find the missing pieces to do that.=<b>[典范计划] 最后部件 - TUED</b>\r\nDISKIO.inc 与 V.L.A.S.T 之间最伟大的合作项目. 由 Kapitel 领导的双方最优秀的工程师和科学家们正在打造一种强大的武器，旨在阻止暴力并夺回旧土. 由于其核心内部的不可思议的力量，典范能够用激光消灭一切，并能制造出极其强大的电磁风暴来摧毁大片区域. 典范还能利用其头部中极其强大的处理器，瓦解周围的一切，引发虚空异常. 一切都很顺利，但有一天抵抗组织成功破坏了典范的建造，导致其在建造过程中被摧毁. 也许它可以被修复并完成，但你需要找到丢失的部件才能做到这一点.

\r\n\r\nLeveling Mod\r\n\r\nUpgrades :\r\n<size%3D75%>Super Strength - Becomes tough - Unlocks at level 3 - Unlocks at chances of 90%.\nUnstabbable - Becomes invulnerable to sharp things - Unlocks at level 1 - Unlocks at chances of 100%.\nNonflammable - Becomes invulnerable to flame - Unlocks at level 2 - Unlocks at chances of 100%.\nUndrownable - Can breath underwater - Unlocks at level 1 - Unlocks at chances of 100%.\nUnbreakable - Can't be broken/sliced - Unlocks at level 5 - Unlocks at chances of 90%.\nUndisintegratable - Can't be disintegrated nor crushed - Unlocks at level 8 - Unlocks at chances of 90%.\nUltra Strength - Becomes so tough that may be immortal - Unlocks at level 10 - Unlocks at chances of 20%.\nSlicing Hand - Turns hands into deadly weapons, can slice anyone. - Unlocks at level 5 - Unlocks at chances of 60%.\n??? - No Description Provided - Unlocks at level 10 - Unlocks at chances of 30%.\nCrushing Hand - Turns hands into deadly weapons, can crush anyone. - Unlocks at level 5 - Unlocks at chances of 60%.\nHealing - Heals every second. - Unlocks at level 7 - Unlocks at chances of 30%.\nInvisibility - Once upgraded, turns invisible forever. - Unlocks at level 3 - Unlocks at chances of 80%.\nGravity Controller - Can change gravity between Moon's Gravity and Earth's - Unlocks at level 7 - Unlocks at chances of 50%.\nUnself - No Description Provided - Unlocks at level ??? - Unlocks at chances of 50%.\n??? - You might die with this - Unlocks at level 15 - Unlocks at chances of 50%.\nBurning Hand - Burns anything you touch (Note : Burning Hand doesn't make you Nonflammable) - Unlocks at level 5 - Unlocks at chances of 70%.\nExtinguisher Hand - Extinguish anything you touch that is on fire - Unlocks at level 1 - Unlocks at chances of 100%.\n??? - Breaks the laws of physics and travels at speed of light to a specific point - Unlocks at level 10 - Unlocks at chances of 100%.\n??? - Travels through time and space. You might end up in a dangerous place - Unlocks at level 15 - Unlocks at chances of 50%.\nFloating - Makes you float in the air forever - Unlocks at level 5 - Unlocks at chances of 80%.\n\r\n\r\n<size%3D100%>More upgrades will be added in next updates!\r\nThanks\r\n-Quan-\r\n                =\r\n\r\n升级模组\r\n\r\n升级项目：\r\n<size%3D75%>超级力量 - 变得坚韧 - 解锁于等级3 - 解锁几率为90%.\n无法刺穿 - 对锋利物品免疫 - 解锁于等级1 - 解锁几率为100%.\n不可燃 - 对火焰免疫 - 解锁于等级2 - 解锁几率为100%.\n无法溺水 - 可以在水下呼吸 - 解锁于等级1 - 解锁几率为100%.\n不可破坏 - 无法被折断或切割 - 解锁于等级5 - 解锁几率为90%.\n不可分解 - 无法被分解或压碎 - 解锁于等级8 - 解锁几率为90%.\n究极力量 - 变得极其坚韧，或许能永生 - 解锁于等级10 - 解锁几率为20%.\n切割之手 - 将双手变成致命武器，可切割任何人 - 解锁于等级5 - 解锁几率为60%.\n??? - 无描述 - 解锁于等级10 - 解锁几率为30%.\n粉碎之手 - 将双手变成致命武器，可粉碎任何人 - 解锁于等级5 - 解锁几率为60%.\n治疗 - 每秒恢复生命 - 解锁于等级7 - 解锁几率为30%.\n隐形 - 升级后永久隐形 - 解锁于等级3 - 解锁几率为80%.\n重力控制器 - 可在月球重力和地球重力之间切换 - 解锁于等级7 - 解锁几率为50%.\n无我 - 无描述 - 解锁于等级 ??? - 解锁几率为50%.\n??? - 使用此能力可能会死亡 - 解锁于等级15 - 解锁几率为50%.\n燃烧之手 - 燃烧你触碰的任何东西（注意：燃烧之手不会让你变得不可燃） - 解锁于等级5 - 解锁几率为70%.\n灭火之手 - 熄灭你触碰到的任何火焰 - 解锁于等级1 - 解锁几率为100%.\n??? - 打破物理法则，以光速移动到特定点 - 解锁于等级10 - 解锁几率为100%.\n??? - 穿越时空. 你可能会出现在危险的地方 - 解锁于等级15 - 解锁几率为50%.\n漂浮 - 让你永久漂浮在空中 - 解锁于等级5 - 解锁几率为80%.\n\r\n\r\n<size%3D100%>更多升级将在后续更新中添加！\r\n感谢\r\n-Quan-\r\n

<b>Firearms Guide</b>\r\nGuide to working Firearms.=<b>枪械指南</b>\r\n可工作枪械的指南. 
Open=打开
<b>Reloading</b>\n1. Right click Firearm, activate <b>Reload</b>\n2. Active the weapon to release magazine/open chamber.\n3. Check what Ammo type the gun Supports.\n4. Go to Ammunition Section and take the ammo magazine the gun supports.\n5. Insert the magazine.\n6. Activate the weapon to cock the chamber.\n<b>Weapon Reloaded!</b>=<b>装弹指南</b>\n1. 右键点击枪械，激活<b>装弹</b>\n2. 激活武器以释放弹匣/打开弹膛. \n3. 检查枪支支持的弹药类型. \n4. 前往弹药部分，拿取枪支支持的弹匣. \n5. 插入弹匣. \n6. 激活武器以拉上枪膛. \n<b>武器已装填！</b>














//121*能力模组重铸_Powers Mod Reforged
Powers Mod Reforged=能力模组重铸
Adds new powers.=添加新能力.
<b>Heal Power Reforged</b>\nHeals all life nearby.=<b>治疗之力 [重铸]</b>\n治疗附近所有生命，恢复生命、治愈骨折、止血补血、解除异常状态.
<b>Pressure Reforged</b>.\n =<b>压力 [重铸]</b>\n向物体施加向下的强力，将其压至地面.
<b>Cure Reforged</b>\nCure all zombies nearby.=<b>治愈 [重铸]</b>\n治愈附近所有僵尸，清除腐烂状态.
<b>Pain Reforged</b>\nInflicts pain to all life nearby.=<b>痛苦 [重铸]</b>\n使附近所有生命感到剧烈痛苦.
<b>Suffocate Reforged</b>\nSuffocates all life nearby.=<b>窒息 [重铸]</b>\n使附近所有生命缺氧窒息（对机器人无效）.
<b>Detach Reforged</b>.\n =<b>分离 [重铸]</b>\n切断目标肢体的骨骼与肌腱，使其脱离.
<b>Acid Reforged</b>\nInflicts acid damage to all life nearby.=<b>强酸 [重铸]</b>\n向附近所有生命注入强酸，造成持续腐蚀伤害.
<b>Crush Power Reforged</b>.\n =<b>粉碎之力 [重铸]</b>\n直接压碎目标的肢体或骨骼.
<b>Head Explosion Reforged</b>.\n =<b>头部爆炸 [重铸]</b>\n单独引爆目标的头部，将其粉碎.
<b>Rot Reforged</b>.\n =<b>腐烂 [重铸]</b>\n加速目标的肉体腐烂进程.
<b>Bone Heal Reforged</b>\nHeals bones.=<b>骨骼治疗 [重铸]</b>\n治愈目标的所有骨折.
<b>Vampire Power Reforged</b>\nRemoves blood.=<b>吸血鬼之力 [重铸]</b>\n持续吸取目标的血液，造成失血伤害.
<b>Charge Reforged</b>.\n =<b>充能 [重铸]</b>\n使物体充满大量静电荷，可电击接触物.
<b>Midas Touch Reforged</b>.\n =<b>点金之手 [重铸]</b>\n将目标变为黄金，冻结并硬化其身体.
<b>Damage Reforged</b>.\n =<b>伤害 [重铸]</b>\n对目标造成持续枪击伤害，不断削弱生命.
<b>Zombie Infection Reforged</b>.\n =<b>僵尸感染 [重铸]</b>\n向目标注入复生代液，使其转变为僵尸.
<b>Fire cannon Reforged</b>.\n =<b>开火 [重铸]</b>\n点燃目标并施加向上冲击力，将其轰飞.
<b>Super Push Reforged</b>.\n =<b>超级推击 [重铸]</b>\n以巨力瞬间推开物体，大幅提升其速度.
<b>Explosion Reforged</b>.\n =<b>爆炸 [重铸]</b>\n在光标位置引发大爆炸，造成范围破坏.
<b>UnFreeze Reforged</b>.\n =<b>解冻 [重铸]</b>\n解除目标受到凝滞血清的冻结状态，恢复行动能力.

//144*简易传送门_SimplePortals
SimplePortals=简易传送门
Adds a portal gun that can create portals.=添加一把可以创建传送门的传送门枪.
<b>Handheld Portal Device [SP]</b>\r\nThe Aperture Science Handheld Portal Device (also known as the Portal Gun, ASHPoD, Aperture Science Quantum Tunneling Device, or ASHPD) is the experimental tool designed to place two portals that objects can pass through. The Handheld Portal Device is designed to create and place portals on immobile surfaces, or surfaces covered with Conversion Gel that are big enough for the Portals to be opened. When the device is fired, a burst of energy will be released from the end of the device. If the projectile strikes a valid surface, a portal of the corresponding color will be formed. If a portal of the other color is already placed, these two portals will be linked. If a portal of the same color is already placed, it will be closed and the new one will be used instead, limiting the player to the use of only two portals at a time. Nothing will happen if a portal is shot at an enemy or other object. The glass chamber and a light on the top of the device will glow with the color of the previously placed portal.=<b>手持传送门装置 [SP]</b>\r\n光圈科技手持传送门装置（也称为传送门枪、ASHPoD、光圈科技量子隧穿装置或ASHPD）是一种实验性工具，旨在创建两个物体可以通过的传送门. 该手持装置设计用于在固定表面或涂有转化凝胶且足够大的表面上创建并放置传送门. 当装置发射时，其末端会释放出一股能量. 如果射弹击中有效的表面，则会形成一个相应颜色的传送门. 如果另一种颜色的传送门已经放置，则这两个传送门将连接起来. 如果相同颜色的传送门已存在，则会关闭旧门并放置新门，限制玩家一次只能使用两个传送门. 如果向敌人或其他物体射击传送门，则不会发生任何事情. 装置顶部的玻璃腔和指示灯会以先前放置的传送门颜色发光. 
<b>Mini Handheld Portal Device [SP]</b>\r\nShoots portals, buy very smol.=<b>迷你手持传送门装置 [SP]</b>\r\n发射传送门，但非常小.

//150*NeitherFishNorCat的共生体_NeitherFishNorCat's Symbiote
\nHow to use:\n1.Find Symbiote in entitiy tab\n2.Place a human near symbiote\n3.The symbiote will attach itself on the human.\n\nControl:\nActivate chest to transform.\nUse click menu to change the color. \nActivate middlebody to release the tentacles. Click menu of middlebody allows you to customize tentacles.\nActivate jaw after transfromation to loose mouth.\nActivate head after transformation to show face.\nUse click menu in hand to activate different abilities. Change the weapon used in weapon ability by using key Y U I O.\nUse click menu of chest to summon 'small venom'\nTransformation regenerates limb.=\n使用方法：\n1. 在实体标签页中找到共生体. \n2. 将人类放置在共生体附近. \n3. 共生体会自动附着在该人类身上. \n\n控制方式：\n激活胸部以变形. \n使用点击菜单更改颜色. \n激活中段躯干以释放触手. 中段躯干的点击菜单允许你自定义触手. \n变形后激活下颚以张开嘴巴. \n变形后激活头部以露出面部. \n使用手部的点击菜单激活不同能力. 按 Y、U、I、O 键更换武器能力中使用的武器. \n使用胸部的点击菜单召唤“小毒液”. \n变形会再生肢体.

//162*蜜蜂实体模组_Bee Entity Mod
Bees Mod=蜜蜂模组
<b>Bee [BeesM]</b>\r\nAn ultra small insect that attacks any entity. Afraid of water, impossible to kill with any weapon. Once the target is lost, it tries to return to the nearest beehive.=<b>蜜蜂 [BeesM]</b>\r\n一种攻击任何实体的超小型昆虫. 怕水，无法用任何武器杀死. 一旦失去目标，它会尝试返回最近的蜂巢
<b>Beekeeper's Mask [BeesM]</b>\r\nWhen wearing it on the head, it protects from bee aggression. To wear a beekeeper's mask, activate it near the head.=<b>养蜂人面具 [BeesM]</b>\r\n戴在头上时可免受蜜蜂攻击. 要戴上养蜂人面具，请在头部附近激活它
<b>Beehive [BeesM]</b>\r\nBee's nest. Creates several dozen bees when activated.=<b>蜂巢 [BeesM]</b>\r\n蜜蜂的巢穴. 激活时会生成数十只蜜蜂








//163*地图碎片
Map Debris=地图碎片
a mod that adds particles to explosions and impacts=一个为爆炸和撞击添加粒子的模组.
<b>Map Debris Settings</b>\r\nEnables or disabled components from the Map Debris Mod.=<b>地图碎片设置</b>\r\n启用或禁用地图碎片模组的组件.
Modify Debris Settings=修改碎片设置
Impacts: True=地图撞击: 开启
Impacts: False=地图撞击: 关闭
Liquid Impacts: True=液体撞击: 开启
Liquid Impacts: False=液体撞击: 关闭
<b>Debris Intensity</b>\r\nModifies the amount of debris per impact / force it requires to make an impact. Higher values will have more frequent and larger debris.=<b>碎片强度</b>\r\n修改每次冲击产生的碎片数量/产生冲击所需的力量. 数值越高，碎片产生越频繁且越大.
Change the intensity of debris=更改碎片强度
higher %3D more frequent and larger=数值越高，碎片出现越频繁且越大.

//165*VIC警察模组_VIC Police Mod
VIC Police Mod=VIC 警察模组
Adds main department of Vicpol, with their kits and weapons and tools, such as PSO, PORT, along with some federal police kits, guns, tasers, batons, bodycam ect and so on.=增加了维多利亚州警察的主要部门，包含他们的装备、武器和工具，例如 PSO、PORT，以及一些联邦警察的装备、枪支、泰瑟枪、警棍、执法记录仪等. 
<size%3D1.5em>VIC Police Mod</size>\nAdds main department of Vicpol, with their kits and weapons and tools, such as PSO, PORT, along with some federal police kits, guns, tasers, batons, bodycam ect and so on.\n<noparse>A mod by culbc for game version 1.11</noparse>=<size%3D1.5em>VIC 警察模组</size>\n增加了维多利亚州警察的主要部门，包含他们的装备、武器和工具，例如 PSO、PORT，以及一些联邦警察的装备、枪支、泰瑟枪、警棍、执法记录仪等. \n<noparse>由 culbc 为游戏版本 1.11 制作的模组</noparse>
<b>VIC PD Mod</b>\r\nyea.=<b>VIC 警察模组</b>\r\n是的.

<b>Protective Services Officers A  PD</b>\r\nPSOs have similar powers to police but they are only allowed to use them when they are on duty in or around ‘designated places’. Like police, PSOs can use reasonable force to do any aspect of their job. This means as much force as is actually necessary to get you to comply with the law.=<b>保护服务官 A PD</b>\r\nPSO拥有与警察相似的权力，但仅限于在“指定地点”内或附近执勤时使用. 与警察一样，PSO可以在执行工作时使用合理武力，即实际所需的必要武力，以确保你遵守法律.

<b>Protective Services Officers B / Summer Alt  PD</b>\r\nPSOs have similar powers to police but they are only allowed to use them when they are on duty in or around ‘designated places’. Like police, PSOs can use reasonable force to do any aspect of their job. This means as much force as is actually necessary to get you to comply with the law.=<b>保护服务官 B / 夏季替换 PD</b>\r\nPSO拥有与警察相似的权力，但仅限于在“指定地点”内或附近执勤时使用. 与警察一样，PSO可以在执行工作时使用合理武力，即实际所需的必要武力，以确保你遵守法律.

<b>Protective Services Officers C / Winter Alt  PD</b>\r\nPSOs have similar powers to police but they are only allowed to use them when they are on duty in or around ‘designated places’. Like police, PSOs can use reasonable force to do any aspect of their job. <b>How To Reload  RFC</b>\r\n- press Y while your mouse is HOVERED over the firearm, you can reload whenever, if the guns empty, full or any.=<b>如何装填 RFC</b>\r\n- 当鼠标悬停在枪械上时按 Y，你可以在任何时候装填，无论枪是空膛、满弹还是任何状态. 

<b>How To Cycle Reload  RFC</b>\r\n- press Y while your mouse is HOVERED over the firearm to CYCLE, you can CYCLE whenever, if the guns empty then press T to RELOAD, you can also RELOAD when ever. If the guns empty and you RELOAD after RELOADING you still need to CYCLE with Y.=<b>如何循环上膛 RFC</b>\r\n- 当鼠标悬停在枪械上时按 Y 进行循环上膛，你可以随时循环. 如果枪是空膛的，按 T 进行装填，你也可以随时装填. 如果枪是空膛的，装填之后你仍然需要用 Y 进行循环上膛.

Adds Power Orbs that can be absorbed by Humans to gain powerful special abilities.=添加了可被人类吸收以获得强大特殊能力的能量宝珠. 
<size%3D1.5em>Power Orbs Mod</size>\nAdds Power Orbs that can be absorbed by Humans to gain silly powerful special abilities.\r\n\r\nMy Discord: https:%2F%2Fdiscord.gg/NY9NdGs388\r\n\r\nAll Power Orbs:\r\n\r\nAqua Orb\r\nCreates a gigant water sphere around the Orb User. If living creatures enter this water sphere, piranhas will spawn and attack that creature. The Orb User can also breath underwater and will not be pushed to the water surface.\r\n\r\nFrost Orb\r\nCreates 5 rotating Ice-Spikes around the Orb User that freeze and heavily damage any creatures on touch. The Orb User also becomes immune against temperature effects.\r\n\r\nPoison Orb\r\nGives the Orb User the ability to automatically shoot many poison projectiles that inflict a bit of acid on anything they hit.\r\n\r\nVoid Orb\r\nGives the Orb User the ability to create Void-Eyes by activating any limb which will start flying and disintegrate anything nearby with a voidbeam.\r\n\r\nExplosion Orb\r\nExplosion-Markes anything alive in a radius. Marked entities explode when leave the zone or when activating the Orb Users Upper-Body. Also makes the Orb User immune to temperature effects and can ignite anything on touch.\r\n\r\nSpace Orb\r\nGives the Orb User the ability to shoot space projectiles from their hands that can trap entities n a dangerous ghostlike state where they will suffocate to death and their body will then split into pieces and get explode.\r\nMAKE IT RAIN BLOOOOOOD!\r\n\r\nGravity Orb\r\nCreates a Gravity Zone around the Orb User that will make anything inside of it weightless. Activate the Orb Users Upper-Body to send a strong gravity-push to everything inside.\r\n\r\nHeaviness Orb\r\nGives the Orb User the ability to shoot a heaviness marking out of his head that will seek out nearby living entities and make them implode.\r\n\r\nWarp Orb\r\nGives the Orb User the ability to shoot warp projectiles that can temporally fade anything they hit. Activate the Orb Users Head to bring back all faded objects and entities with a explosion.\r\n\r\nGilded Orb\r\nGives the Orb User the ability to create a temporary, target seeking gilded sword that will attack any nearby creature by activating the Orb Users Head. Gilded swords have chance to ignite the hit creature and the Orb User will be come invulnerable to temperature effects.\r\n\r\nAll the Orbs give a durability boost to the orb user.\r\nAll powers can be toggled in the context menu.\r\nAll the Orbs are contained in the newly added Category by this Mod.\r\n\r\nv1.2.1=<size%3D1.5em>能量宝珠模组</size>\n添加了可被人类吸收以获得强大特殊能力的能量宝珠. \r\n\r\n我的 Discord：https:%2F%2Fdiscord.gg/NY9NdGs388\r\n\r\n所有能量宝珠：\r\n\r\n流水宝珠\r\n在宝珠使用者周围创造一个巨大的水球. 如果有活物进入这个水球，食人鱼就会生成并攻击该生物. 宝珠使用者还可以在水下呼吸，且不会被推至水面. \r\n\r\n霜冻宝珠\r\n在宝珠使用者周围创造5个旋转的冰刺，触碰时会冻结并重创任何生物. 宝珠使用者还会免疫温度效果. \r\n\r\n剧毒宝珠\r\n赋予宝珠使用者自动发射大量毒液弹丸的能力，对击中的任何目标施加少量酸液效果. \r\n\r\n虚空宝珠\r\n赋予宝珠使用者通过激活任意肢体来创造虚空之眼的能力，虚空之眼会飞行并用虚空光束瓦解附近的一切. \r\n\r\n爆炸宝珠\r\n标记范围内所有活物. 被标记的实体在离开区域或激活宝珠使用者上半身时会爆炸. 同时使宝珠使用者免疫温度效果，并能点燃触碰到的任何东西. \r\n\r\n太空宝珠\r\n赋予宝珠使用者从手中发射太空弹丸的能力，可将实体困在危险的幽灵状态中，使其窒息而死，尸体随后分裂成碎片并爆炸. \r\n让血雨倾盆而下！\r\n\r\n重力宝珠\r\n在宝珠使用者周围创造一个重力场，使其中的一切失重. 激活宝珠使用者上半身可对内部一切施加强力重力推击. \r\n\r\n沉重宝珠\r\n赋予宝珠使用者从头部发射沉重标记的能力，该标记会寻找附近的活体实体并使其内爆. \r\n\r\n扭曲宝珠\r\n赋予宝珠使用者发射扭曲弹丸的能力，可暂时淡化击中的任何目标. 激活宝珠使用者头部可使所有淡化的物体和实体在爆炸中恢复. \r\n\r\n镀金宝珠\r\n赋予宝珠使用者通过激活头部来创造一柄临时的追踪镀金剑，攻击附近的生物. 镀金剑有几率点燃被击中的生物，且宝珠使用者将对温度效果免疫. \r\n\r\n所有宝珠都会为使用者提供耐久度提升. \r\n所有能力都可以在上下文菜单中切换. \r\n所有宝珠都包含在本模组新增的分类中. \r\n\r\nv1.2.1
<b>Power Orbs</b>\r\nAdds Power Orbs lmao.=<b>能量宝珠</b>\r\n添加了能量宝珠，哈哈. 

<b>Aqua Orb</b>\r\nCreates a gigant water sphere around the Orb User. If living creatures enter this water sphere, piranhas will spawn and attack that creature. The Orb User can also breath underwater and will not be pushed to the water surface.=<b>水之宝珠</b>\r\n在宝珠使用者周围创造一个巨大的水球. 如果有活物进入这个水球，食人鱼就会出现并攻击该生物. 宝珠使用者也可以在水下呼吸，并且不会被推向水面.

Also makes the Orb User immune to temperature effects and can ignite anything on touch.=<b>爆炸宝珠</b>\r\n在半径范围内给所有活物施加爆炸标记. 被标记的实体离开该区域或激活宝珠使用者的上半身时会爆炸. 同时使宝珠使用者免疫温度效果，并可在接触时点燃任何物体.

//171*灵魂模组_Souls Mod
<noparse>Souls Mod v1.5</noparse>=<noparse>灵魂模组 v1.5</noparse>
This Mod allows you to extract the soul out of any living entity and transfer it into another enity or sacrefice it to a bunch of ancient shrines and obelisks!=这个模组允许你从任何活体实体中提取灵魂，并将其转移到另一个实体中，或将其献祭给一系列远古神殿和方尖碑！
<size%3D1.5em>Souls Mod v1.5</size>\nThis Mod allows you to extract the soul out of any living entity and transfer it into another enity or sacrefice it to a bunch of ancient shrines and obelisks!\r\n\r\nThis Mod adds:\r\nSoul Extractor: Extracts the soul of an entity by touching its head.\r\n\r\nSoul Returner: Returns a soul back to its current host\r\n\r\nAmulet of Absorbtion: Can absorb other souls to heavily heal and strengthen the wearer.\r\n\r\nAmulet of Protection: Protects a human while wearing from his soul being extracted\r\n\r\nObelisk of Fire: Reqires 4 sacrefices and burns anything in seight on activation.\r\n\r\nObelisk of Frost: Reqires 4 sacrefices and freezes everything in seight on activation.\r\n\r\nShrine of Energy: Reqires 1 sacrefice and lets electricity run through anything nearby but deactivates again after 30 seconds.\r\n\r\nEmpty Vessel: An strong and durable anicent stone golem best used by souls as body.\r\n\r\nAltar of mass extraction: Extracts all souls in range! Needs to be activated by an item with similair properties.\r\n\r\nAnicent Sword of Fire: Requires 1 sacrefice to activate special fire abilities.\r\n\r\nAnicent Sword of Poision: Requires 1 sacrefice to activate special poison/acid abilities.\r\n\r\nAnicent Sword of Tranquility: Requires 1 sacrefice to but entities to sleep and shoot a tranquility spike.\r\n\r\nAncient Voidhammer: Requires 2 sacrefices and can disintegrate and mess up stuff ig.\r\n\r\nSoul Settings: Opens a config menu where you can change if souls should automaticly come out of their bodys on death and other things like android possesion.\r\n\r\n\r\nEverything is in the new Souls Mod Category.\r\nOnly the core of a soul can interact with the mortal world.\r\nEvery entity has its unique soul that can be transfered or stuff.\r\n\r\nv1.5=<size%3D1.5em>灵魂模组 v1.5</size>\n这个模组允许你从任何活体实体中提取灵魂，并将其转移到另一个实体中，或将其献祭给一系列远古神殿和方尖碑！\r\n\r\n此模组添加了：\r\n灵魂提取器：通过触碰实体头部来提取其灵魂. \r\n\r\n灵魂归还器：将灵魂归还至其当前宿主. \r\n\r\n吸收护符：可以吸收其他灵魂来大量治疗和强化佩戴者. \r\n\r\n保护护符：佩戴时保护人类，防止其灵魂被提取. \r\n\r\n火焰方尖碑：需要 4 次献祭，激活后燃烧视野内的一切. \r\n\r\n霜冻方尖碑：需要 4 次献祭，激活后冻结视野内的一切. \r\n\r\n能量神殿：需要 1 次献祭，让电流流过附近的一切，但 30 秒后再次关闭. \r\n\r\n空容器：一个强大耐久的远古石魔像，最适合灵魂作为身体使用. \r\n\r\n大规模提取祭坛：提取范围内的所有灵魂！需要用具有相似属性的物品激活. \r\n\r\n远古火焰之剑：需要 1 次献祭来激活特殊火焰能力. \r\n\r\n远古毒剑：需要 1 次献祭来激活特殊毒液/酸液能力. \r\n\r\n远古宁静之剑：需要 1 次献祭来让实体陷入沉睡并发射宁静尖刺. \r\n\r\n远古虚空锤：需要 2 次献祭，可以瓦解和搞乱东西. \r\n\r\n灵魂设置：打开一个配置菜单，你可以在此更改灵魂是否应在死亡时自动离开身体，以及机器人附身等其他设置. \r\n\r\n\r\n所有内容都在新的灵魂模组分类中. \r\n只有灵魂的核心才能与凡间世界互动. \r\n每个实体都有其独特的灵魂，可以转移或做其他事情. \r\n\r\nv1.5

//180*鱼的黑魔法
<noparse>Fish Black Magic </noparse>=<noparse>鱼的黑魔法</noparse>
Inspired by an old song <That Old Black Magic>=灵感来自一首老歌《That Old Black Magic》
<size%3D1.5em>Fish Black Magic </size>\nInspired by an old song <That Old Black Magic>\n<noparse>A mod by NeitherFishNorCat for game version 1.21+</noparse>=<size%3D1.5em>鱼的黑魔法</size>\n灵感来自歌曲 "That Old Black Magic"\r\n\r\n包含五种不同的魔法和一些独特的魔法物品，每种物品都属于Black Magic类别下. \r\n\r\n如何学习魔法：\r\n1. 放置一个祭坛\r\n2. 在祭坛上放 6 根蜡烛\r\n3. 将祭坛物品放在祭坛的桌子部分\r\n4. 在祭坛上放置人类\r\n5. 激活祭坛\r\n\r\n魔法类型：\r\n血魔法 - 血挪移和血液抽取，激活中间身体开始抽取血液. 在抽取血液的同时，激活他的手并指向其他人进行血挪移. 进行血液抽取时，血魔法使用者可以通过触碰造成伤口\r\n使用带血状态的祭祀刀作为祭坛物品\r\n\r\n巫毒魔法 - 使用玩偶来转换伤害，激活他的手部然后触摸玩偶以获得一个大玩偶，然后激活玩偶的中间身体并将其与其他人类相连接以造成伤害转移. 对玩偶使用蜘蛛和青蛙会有特殊效果\r\n将玩偶用作祭坛道具\r\n\r\n死灵法术 - 召唤鬼魂附在尸体上，激活他的手召唤鬼魂，鬼魂可被玫瑰吸收\r\n使用头骨作为祭坛物品\r\n\r\n镜像魔法 - 在镜像世界和现实世界之间切换，这个功能不太稳定慎用\r\n使用玫瑰作为祭坛物品\r\n\r\n变身魔法 - 将人类变为动物，只有死亡或亲吻才能解除诅咒. 如果使用亲吻来打破诅咒，亲吻的两人将坠入爱河\r\n使用皇冠作为祭坛物品\r\n\r\n每种魔法都以血液抽取为基础魔法，通过抽取血液可获得魔法能量，血液只能从伤口和容器中抽取\r\n\r\n\r\n魔法道具：\r\n冰冻之心 - 逆向炎拳\r\n\r\n被诅咒的南瓜 - 南瓜会对触碰它的人下诅咒. 诅咒包含一个倒计时，一旦倒计时结束，这个人就会变成另一个南瓜. 人类可以通过接触其他人类来传递诅咒. \r\n\r\n玫瑰 - 存储灵魂，可用于使任意物体被附体并变成自主行动的“活物”\r\n\r\n丘比特箭 - 将箭同时插入两个不同的人体内，就会产生爱情. \r\n\r\n魔镜 - 激活魔镜可切换世界，通过魔镜快速移动物体可将其传送到相反的世界. \r\n\r\n特有机制：\r\n爱情 - 相当于狼人杀里的恋人. \r\n\r\n镜像世界 - 通过镜子与现实世界相连的平行世界\n<noparse>由 NeitherFishNorCat 制作的模组，适用于游戏版本 1.21+</noparse>

For additional offensive power, the bikaku kagune of the Bin brothers can be projected from the spearhead, spiraling around it in a drill-like manner.=<b>[SS级] 堂岛</b>\r\n堂岛1/2经由真户晓和地行甲乙使用“瓶”兄弟的赫子修复，呈锥形枪头长矛形态. 可额外从枪尖释放“瓶”兄弟的尾赫，如钻头般螺旋缠绕增强攻击力. 
<b>[SS Rank] Jason13</b>\r\nRinkaku quinque that takes the form of a square and jagged scythe and has an L-shaped blade with a sharp tip. It was created from Yamori's kakuhou and its final form was designed by Kouitsu Chigyou of the CCG Laboratory Division.=<b>[SS级] 杰森13</b>\r\n鳞赫库因克，呈方形锯齿镰刀形态，带有L型利刃和尖锐尖端. 由“壁虎”的赫包制成，最终形态由CCG实验课的地行甲乙设计. 
<b>[SS Rank] Kajiri</b>\r\nA unique quinque with a double-bladed design. Press F to shoot crystals.=<b>[SS级] 梶理</b>\r\n独特的双刃型库因克. 按F键发射结晶. 
<b>[SSS Rank] Narukami</b>\r\nNarukami is an ukaku-type quinque with a firing rate of four firing patterns. It has a great range but only limited ammunition capacity. Created from the kakuhou of an SSS rated ghoul.=<b>[SSS级] 鸣神</b>\r\n鸣神为羽赫库因克，拥有四种射击模式. 射程极远但弹容量有限. 由SSS级喰种的赫包制成. 
<b>[SSS Rank] Owl Quinque</b>\r\nA quinque owned by Arima and created from a kakuhou torn out during his battle with the Non-Killing Owl. It is the only known example of an SSS-rated quinque, and the only one known to be created from a living ghoul.=<b>[SSS级] 枭·库因克</b>\r\n有马所持有的库因克，由与“不杀之枭”战斗中夺取的赫包制成. 是已知唯一的SSS级库因克，也是唯一已知由活体喰种制成的库因克. 
<b><color%3D#6F1C1C>RC Cell [Owl]</color></b>\r\nYoshimura preset. Starts at rank SSS with Owl full kakuja available.=<b><color%3D#6F1C1C>RC细胞 [枭]</color></b>\r\n芳村预设. 初始SSS级，可使用枭·完整赫者形态. 
<b><color%3D#9966CC>RC Cell [Tsukiyama]</color></b>\r\nShuu Tsukiyama preset. Starts at rank S with a Koukaku ghoul kagune.=<b><color%3D#9966CC>RC细胞 [月山]</color></b>\r\n月山习预设. 初始S级，甲赫喰种赫子. 
<b><color%3D#9B111E>RC Cell [Noro]</color></b>\r\nNoro preset. Starts at rank SSS with extreme durability and Noro bikaku.=<b><color%3D#9B111E>RC细胞 [诺罗]</color></b>\r\n诺罗预设. 初始SSS级，拥有极高耐久度与诺罗式尾赫. 
<b><color%3D#9FB7B8>CRC Gas Grenade</color></b>\r\nDeploys a CRC cloud. Ghouls inside cannot regenerate or activate Kagune.=<b><color%3D#9FB7B8>CRC瓦斯手雷</color></b>\r\n释放CRC气体云. 处于其中的喰种无法再生或激活赫子. 
<b><color%3D#A54CFF>RC Cell [Ayato]</color></b>\r\nAyato Kirishima preset. Starts at rank S with anime-colored ukaku wings and crystal attacks.=<b><color%3D#A54CFF>RC细胞 [绫人]</color></b>\r\n雾岛绫人预设. 初始S级，动画配色羽赫双翼，可进行结晶攻击. 
<b><color%3D#B08A62>Anteiku Coffee</color></b>\r\nA bitter cup from Anteiku. Calms Madness and memory pressure.=<b><color%3D#B08A62>古董咖啡</color></b>\r\n来自古董的一杯苦咖啡. 可安抚疯狂与记忆压力. 
<b><color%3D#B14B32>Ghoul Meat</color></b>\r\nA compact meat source for ghouls. Touch a ghoul to fully restore hunger.=<b><color%3D#B14B32>喰种肉</color></b>\r\n便携式喰种肉源. 触碰喰种即可完全恢复饥饿值. 
<b><color%3D#B8B8B8>RC Suppressant Syringe</color></b>\r\nSuppresses ghoul regeneration, Kagune, and Kakuja for 30 seconds.=<b><color%3D#B8B8B8>RC抑制注射器</color></b>\r\n30秒内抑制喰种的再生、赫子与赫者化能力. 
<b><color%3D#C43A3A>RC Cell [Jason]</color></b>\r\nRinkaku preset of Yamori. Starts at rank S with two oversized tentacles and Jason half-kakuja lineage.=<b><color%3D#C43A3A>RC细胞 [杰森]</color></b>\r\n“壁虎”鳞赫预设. 初始S级，拥有两根巨大触手及杰森半赫者谱系. 
<b><color%3D#CC6633>RC Cell [Bin]</color></b>\r\nBin brothers preset. Starts at rank S with Bin bikaku and no kakuja forms.=<b><color%3D#CC6633>RC细胞 [瓶]</color></b>\r\n“瓶”兄弟预设. 初始S级，持有“瓶”式尾赫，无赫者形态. 
<b><color%3D#D8D8D8>Enable/Disable Hunger</color></b>\r\nUse to toggle ghoul hunger globally. Press F to toggle.=<b><color%3D#D8D8D8>启用/禁用饥饿</color></b>\r\n用于全局切换喰种饥饿状态. 按F键切换. 
<b><color%3D#D95B5B>RC Cell [Nishio]</color></b>\r\nNishio preset. Starts at rank A with Nishio bikaku.=<b><color%3D#D95B5B>RC细胞 [西尾]</color></b>\r\n西尾预设. 初始A级，持有西尾式尾赫. 
<b><color%3D#D9D3C3>CCG Application</color></b>\r\nTurns a human into a Rank 3 CCG investigator on contact.=<b><color%3D#D9D3C3>CCG入职申请书</color></b>\r\n触碰后使人类成为三等CCG搜查官. 
<b><color%3D#E44747>Kakuja Unlock Pill</color></b>\r\nA capsule containing highly concentrated RC cells and mutation catalysts. Upon ingestion, it triggers a sharp RC surge and activates Kakuja mode.=<b><color%3D#E44747>赫者解锁药丸</color></b>\r\n含有高浓度RC细胞与变异催化剂的胶囊. 服用后将引发RC剧烈激增，激活赫者模式. 
<b><color%3D#E6DFC9>Promotion Document</color></b>\r\nPromotes a CCG investigator by one rank on contact.=<b><color%3D#E6DFC9>晋升文件</color></b>\r\n触碰后使CCG搜查官晋升一级. 
<b><color%3D#F25AA8>RC Cell [Rize]</color></b>\r\nRize Kamishiro preset. Starts at rank SS with Ken-style rinkaku and Kaneki kakuja lineage.=<b><color%3D#F25AA8>RC细胞 [利世]</color></b>\r\n神代利世预设. 初始SS级，拥有金木式鳞赫及金木赫者谱系.

<b><color%3D#FF92C2>RC Cell [Kosatka]</color></b>\r\nKosatka preset. Starts at rank SS with reinforced body proportions and tougher limbs.=<b><color%3D#FF92C2>RC细胞 [虎鲸]</color></b>\r\n虎鲸预设. 初始SS级，强化体魄与更坚韧的四肢. 
<b><color%3D#FFB347>RC Booster</color></b>\r\nAdds 1000 RC cells to a ghoul or half-ghoul on contact.=<b><color%3D#FFB347>RC增幅剂</color></b>\r\n触碰后为喰种或半喰种增加1000个RC细胞. 
<b><color%3Dblue>RC Cell [Koukaku]</color></b>\r\nA living RC cell cluster of the Koukaku type. Touch it to a human to transform them into a Koukaku ghoul.=<b><color%3Dblue>RC细胞 [甲赫]</color></b>\r\n甲赫型活体RC细胞集群. 触碰人类可将其转化为甲赫喰种. 
<b><color%3Dgreen>RC Cell [Bikaku]</color></b>\r\nA living RC cell cluster of the Bikaku type. Touch it to a human to transform them into a Bikaku ghoul.=<b><color%3Dgreen>RC细胞 [尾赫]</color></b>\r\n尾赫型活体RC细胞集群. 触碰人类可将其转化为尾赫喰种.

//189*传说之下重制版2.0_Soul Mod Rewrite [2.0.0]
<noparse>Soul Mod Rewrite [2.0.0]</noparse>=<noparse>灵魂模组重制版 [2.0.0]</noparse>
Adds humans with SOULs from UNDERTALE. Select me and read the description for more details! ------>>=添加了来自《传说之下》的拥有灵魂的人类. 选择我并阅读描述以了解更多详情！------>>
<size%3D1.5em>Soul Mod Rewrite [2.0.0]</size>\n<align%3D"center"><size%3D200%><b>SOUL MOD REWRITE</align></size></b>\r\n\r\nThis mod is a rewrite of my old mod that was made a long long time ago. Using my newly found skills, and my determination, I created this.\r\n\r\n<align%3D"center"><size%3D150%><b>MAIN FEATURES</b></align></size>\r\n\r\nAdds humans with different SOULs, with customizable colors in the context menu.\r\n\r\nFUN values were removed.\r\n\r\nIf a human's SOUL is <b>not</b> white, they have the ability to <color%3D"yellow">SAVE</color>, <color%3D"yellow">LOAD</color>, and <color%3D"yellow">RESET</color>.\r\nWhite SOULs cannot do anything. When it dies, it will fade into dust, leaving no trace of existing.\r\nNon-white SOULs have a chance to refuse their SOUL upon death. White SOULs cannot do this.\r\n<color%3D"red">RED</color> SOULs can sometimes be extremely determined, and will resist death.\r\nYou are able to manually <color%3D"red">REFUSE</color> any non-white SOUL that is cracked via the context menu.\r\nYou can adjust the chance that humans refuse via the context menu. (1 - 100) The number chosen will be a 1 in ## chance to refuse.\r\n\r\nUsing the context menu, you can rip SOULs from humans and put them into other humans or SOUL containers.\r\n\r\n<align%3D"center"><b><size%3D100%>CREDITS</b></align></size>\r\nOriginal Mod, Sprites ------ ME because I made it.\r\nSounds, Ideas, Sprite Bases ------ UNDERTALE\r\nIdeas, Sounds ------ UNDERTALE <color%3D"yellow">YELLOW</color>\r\n\r\nArmor Structure ------ weirdo's Functioning Armor\r\nDisplay Text Font Source ------ MaxDux and QuanGPT's Chatterbox Mod=<size%3D1.5em>灵魂模组重制版 [2.0.0]</size>\n<align%3D"center"><size%3D200%><b>灵魂模组重制版</align></size></b>\r\n\r\n这个模组是我很久以前制作的旧模组的重制版. 运用我新学到的技能和我的决心，我创造了这个模组. \r\n\r\n<align%3D"center"><size%3D150%><b>主要特性</b></align></size>\r\n\r\n添加了拥有不同灵魂的人类，可在上下文菜单中自定义颜色. \r\n\r\nFUN值已被移除. \r\n\r\n如果人类的灵魂<b>不是</b>白色的，他们就有能力<color%3D"yellow">保存</color>、<color%3D"yellow">读取</color>和<color%3D"yellow">重置</color>. \r\n白色灵魂无法做任何事情. 当其死亡时，会化为尘埃，不留任何存在痕迹. \r\n非白色灵魂在死亡时有几率拒绝死亡. 白色灵魂无法做到这一点. \r\n<color%3D"red">红色</color>灵魂有时会极其坚定，并能抵抗死亡. \r\n你可以通过上下文菜单手动<color%3D"red">拒绝</color>任何已碎裂的非白色灵魂. \r\n你可以通过上下文菜单调整人类拒绝的几率. （1 - 100）所选数字将成为 ## 分之一（1 in ##）的拒绝几率. \r\n\r\n使用上下文菜单，你可以从人类身上撕下灵魂并将其放入其他人类或灵魂容器中. \r\n\r\n<align%3D"center"><b><size%3D100%>致谢</b></align></size>\r\n原始模组、精灵图 ------ 我本人，因为我制作了它. \r\n音效、创意、精灵图基础 ------ 《传说之下》\r\n创意、音效 ------ 《传说之下<color%3D"yellow">黄色</color>》\r\n\r\n铠甲结构 ------ weirdo的Functioning Armor\r\n显示文本字体来源 ------ MaxDux和QuanGPT的Chatterbox Mod
